TITLE      Atlas of neutron resonances resonance parameters and   V100100100003 
            thermal cross sections Z=1-100                        V100100100004 
AUTHOR     (S.F.Mughabghab)                                       V100100100005 
INSTITUTE  (1USABNL)                                              V100100100006 
REFERENCE  (B,NEUT.RES,,2006)                                     V100100100007 
REL-REF    (E,,S.F.Mughabghab+,B,NEUT.CS 1A,,1981)                V100100100008 
           (E,,S.F.Mughabghab,B,NEUT.CS 1B,,1984)                 V100100100009 
           (O,V1002001,S.F.Mughabghab,B,NEUT.RES,,2006)           V100100100010 
           Second  part of the compilation from the same book     V100100100011 
METHOD     Evaluation: The experimental results for nuclei        V100100100012 
            between H and Fm were critically surveyed,            V100100100013 
            renormalized and resonance parameters were deduced.   V100100100014 
           Cross sections and resonance integrals were given      V100100100015 
            where available, otherwise they were calculated using V100100100016 
            the resonance parameter data.                         V100100100017 
ANALYSIS   Resonance parameters and cross sections were analyzed  V100100100018 
            using Atlas codes.                                    V100100100019 
           The neutron radiative cross sections were measured in  V100100100020 
            a Maxwellian flux, other measurements are commented.  V100100100021 
           Scattering length (coherent amplitude) b is related to V100100100022 
            elastic scattering cross section as follows:          V100100100023 
             sigma=4pi x b**2.                                    V100100100024 
            Both values are based on independent measurements.    V100100100025 
           Resonance integrals (RI) are based on experimental     V100100100026 
            values, if no measurements then calculated from       V100100100027 
            resonance parameter values from 0.5 eV to highest     V100100100028 
            energy of the resolved resonance region.              V100100100029 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) S.F. Mughabghab tabulated total errors for     V100100100030 
            integral values.                                      V100100100031 
ADD-RES    The Atlas also contains vast resonance parameter data, V100100100032 
            however, it is next to impossible to compile it       V100100100033 
            manually and Elsevier copyright agreement prevents    V100100100034 
            any usage of electronic files.                        V100100100035
